\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00590}00590\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Since\ this\ is\ a\ branchless\ decoder,\ four\ bytes\ will\ be\ read\ from\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00591}00591\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ buffer\ regardless\ of\ the\ actual\ length\ of\ the\ next\ character.\ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00592}00592\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ means\ the\ buffer\ \_must\_\ have\ at\ least\ three\ bytes\ of\ zero\ padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00593}00593\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ following\ the\ end\ of\ the\ data\ stream.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00594}00594\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00596}00596\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ character\ was\ somehow\ invalid:\ invalid\ byte\ sequence,\ non-\/canonical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00597}00597\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ encoding,\ or\ a\ surrogate\ half.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00600}00600\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ occurs,\ this\ pointer\ will\ be\ a\ guess\ that\ depends\ on\ the\ particular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00601}00601\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ error,\ but\ it\ will\ always\ advance\ at\ least\ one\ byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00602}00602\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
